### BREAKING CHANGES

* **kengine-breadcrumbs-item:** BreadcrumbsItem's stableDomRef property has been removed - use
getDomRef to get the matching actual DOM ref
* The icons SVG imports are changed. If you previously had
```js
import "@kengine/webcomponents-icons/dist/accept.svg";
```
 you have to import the SVGs from the **v4/**  or the **v5/** directory:
```js
import "@kengine/webcomponents-icons/dist/v4/accept.svg"; //  for KHULNASOFTIcons4.0
import "@kengine/webcomponents-icons/dist/v5/accept.svg"; // for KHULNASOFTIcons5.0
```
* **kengine-message-strip:** MessageStrip component's tag name has been renamed from kengine-messagestrip to kengine-message-strip.
* **kengine-input:** The "suggestion-scroll" event has been removed as there is no such UX specified.
* **kengine-color-palette-popover:** The selected color is now available as it is documented: event.detail.color

* **kengine-combobox:** filter value property is removed.

* **kengine-input:** The highlight property is removed and the feature is enabled by default

### BREAKING CHANGES

* **kengine-busyindicator:** Medium size is now default

FIXES: https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/issues/1337
* **kengine-mcb-item:** - kengine-multi-combobox no longer accepts `kengine-li` for items use `kengine-multi-combobox-item` instead.
- **kengine-combobox-item:** change the tag name from `kengine-combobox-item` to `kengine-cb-item`
* **kengine-tabcontainer:** `itemSelect` is renamed to `tabSelect` and the `item` event param is renamed to `tab`.

* **kengine-card:** the proeprty `subtitle` has been renamed to `subheading`
* **kengine-textarea:** The property `maxLength` has been renamed to `maxlength`and the attribute name is changed from `max-length` to `maxlength`.

### Code Refactoring
* **kengine-shellbar:** move component to @kengine/webcomponents-fiori package ([#887](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/pull/887)) ([06f1770](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/commit/17c25ff123436c1f6e11513055b33977b06f1770))
* **kengine-card:** replace "avatar" property with "avatar" slot ([#928](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/issues/928)) ([0489673](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/commit/0489673))
* **kengine-shellbar:** rename "icon" slot to "startButton" ([#901](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/issues/901)) ([5ca3280](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/commit/5ca3280))
* **kengine-shellbar-item:** "src" property renamed to "name" ([#928](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/pull/928)) ([8e060d1](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/commit/0489673610ce2fd0e96d0a3a1f4e0465d8e060d1))
* **kengine-shellbar:** extract animated co-pilot SVG as add-on asset ([#904](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/pull/904)) ([c25e0a7](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/commit/59fead49d7a3222d55270584bb048190dc25e0a7))

### BREAKING CHANGES

* **icons:** Move all individual icons to a new npm package called `@kengine/webcomponents-icons`.

You have to install the package 
```js
npm i @kengine/webcomponents-icons --save
```
The import statements should be changed

Before:
```js
@kengine/webcomponents/dist/icons/add.js
```

After:
```js
@kengine/webcomponents-icons/dist/add.js
```
* **kengine-shellbar:** move component to new `@kengine/webcomponents-fiori` package ([#887](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/pull/887)) ([06f1770](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/commit/17c25ff123436c1f6e11513055b33977b06f1770))

* **kengine-shellbar:** rename "icon" slot to "startButton" ([#901](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/issues/901)) ([5ca3280](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/commit/5ca3280))

The slot accepts a kengine-button and overstyles it to match ShellBar's styling.

* **kengine-shellbar:** extract animated co-pilot SVG as add-on asset ([#904](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/pull/904)) ([c25e0a7](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/commit/59fead49d7a3222d55270584bb048190dc25e0a7))

To get the ShellBar's coPilot animated you have to import the `@kengine/webcomponents-fiori/dist/features/CoPilotAnimation.js` module

* **kengine-shellbar-item:** "src" property renamed to "name" ([#928](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/pull/928)) ([8e060d1](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/commit/0489673610ce2fd0e96d0a3a1f4e0465d8e060d1))

The "src" property was renamed to icon and accepts icon name (such as "add") instead of icon src (such as "sap-icon://add")

* **kengine-card:** replace "avatar" property with "avatar" slot ([#928](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/issues/928)) ([0489673](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/commit/0489673))

The avatar property was removed.
Use the avatar slot instead - pass an icon(<kengine-icon) or an image(<img).

Before:
```html
<kengine-card avatar="sap-icon://add"></kengine-card>
```

After:
```html
<kengine-card><kengine-icon name="add" slot="avatar"></kengine-icon></kengine-card>`
```
and respectively:
```html
<kengine-card avatar="http://url/to/my/image"></kengine-card>`
```
becomes:
```html
<kengine-card><img src="http://url/to/my/image" slot="avatar"/></kengine-card>`
```

* **kengine-icon:** "src" property was renamed to "name".

The "name" poperty accepts icon name (such as "add") instead of icon src (such as "sap-icon://add").
Note: the src property will continue to work until the next release due to the impact of the change, but will produce a warning in the console.

### BREAKING CHANGES

* **kengine-popover:** stayOpenOnScroll is now removed
Popover will no longer close when the browser is scrolled
and its parent (opener) is visible in the viewport.
* **kengine-li:** CSS variable --kengine-listitem-background-color is removed,
set the desired background directly on the tag.
* **kengine-table:** width property of the kengine-table-column has been removed, use CSS to give width to the columns.
`<kengine-table-column style="width: 100px">...`
* **kengine-multi-combobox:** property validate-input is removed,
use the property allow-custom-values, note built in validation is enabled by default.





# [1.0.0-rc.2](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/compare/v1.0.0-rc.1...v1.0.0-rc.2) (2019-07-04)

### Bug Fixes

* **popup:** remove body styles in onExitDOM ([#593](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/issues/593)) ([410b8f6](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/commit/410b8f6))

### Code Refactoring

* **kengine-shellbar-item:** Rename press event to itemClick ([#606](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/issues/606)) ([5bfab39](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/commit/5bfab39))
* **kengine-popover, kengine-dialog**: remove noHeader property (#615) ([6a990a7](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/commit/6a990a7)), closes [#615](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/issues/615)


### BREAKING CHANGES

* **kengine-shellbar-item:** kengine-shellbar-item press event is renamed to itemClick
* **kengine-popover, kengine-dialog**: the property noHeader is removed, the presence of header is based on the values of "headerText" property and "header" slot

### Code Refactoring

* **kengine-button:** rename type property to design ([#504](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/issues/504)) ([a62b471](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/commit/a62b471))

### BREAKING CHANGES

* the parameter of the change event is now called "selectedOption"; kengine-select enforces kengine-option as children in the metadata
* **kengine-select:** Use kengine-option instead of kengine-li in kengine-select
* **kengine-link:** property type is renamed to design
* **kengine-button:** type property is changed to design
* **kengine-switch:** type property is renamed to boolean property graphical
* **kengine-messagestrip:** hideIcon property is renamed to noIcon
* **kengine-popover:** hideArrow property is renamed to noArrow
* **kengine-popover:** hideHeader property renamed to noHeader

### Features

* **kengine-list:** selectionChange event provides previousSelection items ([#418](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/issues/418)) ([f0fc8f2](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/commit/f0fc8f2))

### BREAKING CHANGES

* **kengine-list:** the "selectionChange" event param "items" has been renamed to "selectedItems".
* **kengine-list:** the "backgroundDesign" property has been removed, use the corresponding
CSS variable (--_kengine_listitem_background_color) to alter the list items` background.
* **kengine-panel:** the "backgroundDesign" property has been removed, use the corresponding
CSS variables (--_kengine_panel_background_color) to alter the panel background.
* **kengine-datepicker:** 'liveChange' event has been renamed to 'input'.
* **kengine-checkbox:** property "readOnly" has been renamed to "readonly".
* **kengine-radiobutton:** property "readOnly" has been renamed to "readonly".

* provide named exports for some base modules ([#347](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/issues/347)) ([2e2439a](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/commit/2e2439a))
* **kengine-shellbar:** adds logoPress and coPilotPress events ([#301](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/issues/301)) ([f221123](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/commit/f221123))
* **kengine-shellbar:** menuItems slot and menuItemPress event ([#317](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/issues/317)) ([f24f78b](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/commit/f24f78b))


### BREAKING CHANGES

* **kengine-timeline:** 'timestamp' and 'timeFormat'  properties are removed.
Instead use subtitle-text property and directly format the text as
desired.
* the kengine-toolbar component is removed, we recommend using div or similar HTML tag in combination with flex instead.
* **kengine-panel:** the expand event is removed, use the toggle event instead.
* **kengine-tabcontainer:** 'headerMode' property is removed. All Tabs by Fiori guidelines are rendered in
inline mode
* **kengine-tabcontainer:** 'headerBackgroundDesign' property is removed
* **kengine-tabcontainer:** 'backgroundDesign' property is removed
* **kengine-tabcontainer:** 'content' property is removed. Instead if you want to use the TabContainer as
a filter just use it with 'collapsed' set to true and 'fixed' set to true
* **kengine-tabcontainer:** 'TabContainerDensityMode' is deleted. To set different size modes use ?sap-ui-compactSize=true
* **kengine-tabcontainer:** 'selectedIndex' property is removed. Instead use 'selected' property of the Tab
* **kengine-tabcontainer:** Tab's 'count' property is removed. Instead use the additional-text property
* **kengine-tabcontainer:** Tab's 'design' property is removed
* **kengine-shellbar:** titlePress event is removed and replaced by menuItems slot.
* **base:** All files required from the base now have different
path. sap/ui/webcomponents/base/ is removed.

old: @kengine/webcomponents-base/src/sap/ui/webcomponents/base/WebComponent
new: @kengine/webcomponents-base/src/WebComponent




# [0.9.0](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/compare/v0.8.0...v0.9.0) (2019-03-18)


### Features

* **kengine-messagestrip:** initial implementation ([#80](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/issues/80)) ([cbc9c75](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/commit/cbc9c75))


### Bug Fixes

### Code Refactoring

* **kengine-input:** fire input, instead of liveChange ([#159](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/issues/159)) ([b8d978a](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/commit/b8d978a))


### BREAKING CHANGES

* **kengine-input:** liveChange event is no longer fired, listen for the input event instead.

### BREAKING CHANGES

* any applications that wants to support Edge and/or IE11 should now import the respective browser support module. For details, see the [README.md](/README.md#browser-support)
* **kengine-tabcontainer:** The TabContainer "selected-key" and Tab "key" properties are removed. Use TabContainer "selectedIndex" property (selected-index attribute) to set and get the selected tab.
* addCustomCSS is no longer on the Core object. Use Theming instead. [#58](https://github.com/khulnasoft-lab/kengine-webcomponents/pull/58)
